`back-to-profile` → `url_for('profile_page')`\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas\n\n### 1. `data/users.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-separated):\n  1. `username` (str)\n  2. `email` (str)\n  3. `phone` (str)\n  4. `address` (str)\n- Description: User profile information.\n- Examples:\n  - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`\n  - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`\n\n### 2. `data/books.txt`\n- Fields (pipe-separated):\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `title` (str)\n  3. `author` (str)\n  4. `isbn` (str)\n  5. `genre` (str)\n  6. `publisher` (str)\n  7. `year` (int)\n  8. `description` (str)\n  9. `status` (str: Available, Borrowed, Reserved)\n  10. `avg_rating` (float)\n- Description: Book details.\n- Examples:\n  - Schuster|2011|Biography of Apple co-founder.|Available|4.3\n\n### 3. borrowings.txt\n- Path: data/borrowings.txt\n- Fields (pipe '|' delimited):\n  1. borrow_id (int)\n  2. username (str)\n  3. delimited):\n  1. reservation_id (int)\n  2. username (str)\n  3. book_id (int)\n  4. reservation_date (str YYYY-MM-DD)\n  5. status (str) - Values: Active, Cancelled\n- Description: Tracks user reservations for books.\n- Example Rows:\n  - 1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active\n  - 2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Path: data/reviews.txt\n- Fields (pipe '|' delimited):\n Rows:\n  - 1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! profile information.\n- Example Rows:\n  - john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St\n  - jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St\n\n### 2. books.txt\n- Path: data/books.txt\n- Fields Values: Available, Borrowed, Reserved\n  10. avg_rating (float)\n- Description: Stores detailed book information.\n- Example Rows:\n  - 1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8\n  - 2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6\n  - 3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7\n  - 4|The Selfish Gene|Richard Schuster|2011|Biography of Apple co-founder.|Available|4.3\n\n### 3. borrowings.txt\n- Path: data/borrowings.txt\n- Fields (pipe '|' delimited):\n  1. borrow_id (int)\n  2. username (str)\n  3. reservations for books.\n- Example Rows:\n  - 1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active\n  - 2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- Path: data/reviews.txt\n- Fields (pipe '|' delimited):\n  1. review_id (int)\n  2. username (str)\n  3. book_id (int)\n  4. rating (int 1-5)\n  5. review_text (str)\n  6. review_date (str YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Description: Stores user reviews on books.\n- Example Rows:\n  - 1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! A must-read.|2024-11-03\n  - 2|john_reader|3|4|Thought-provoking and eerily relevant today.|2024-10-20\n\n### 6. fines.txt\n- Path: data/fines.txt\n- Fields (pipe '|' delimited):\n  1. fine_id (int)\n  2. username (str)\n  3. borrow_id (int)\n  4. amount (float)\n  5. status (str) - Values: Unpaid, Paid\n  6. date_issued (str YYYY-MM-DD)\n- Description: Records overdue fines issued to users.\n- Example Rows:\n  - 1|john_reader|3|5.00|Unpaid|2024-10-30\n\n---\n\nThis design specification document comprehensively defines the backend Flask routes, frontend HTML template structures, and local text file data schemas for the OnlineLibrary application. This enables parallel and consistent development by frontend and backend teams without ambiguity.\n",

`username` : `str` (current logged-in username)\n\n### Book Catalog Page\n- **URL Path:** `/catalog`\n- **Function Name:** `book_catalog_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `borrow_id` : `int`\n  - `book_title` : `str`\n  - `return_date` : `str` (current date, YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `confirmation_message` : `str`\n\n### My Reservations Page\n- **URL Path:** `/my_reservations`\n- **Function Name:** `my_reservations_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `my_reservations.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reservations` : `list` of `dict` containing:\n    - `reservation_id` : `int`\n    - `book_title` : `str`\n    - `reservation_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `status` : `str` (\"Active\", \"Cancelled\")\n\n### Cancel Reservation Route\n- **URL Path:** `/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `cancel_reservation`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Confirmation or redirect\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reservation_id` : `int`\n  - `confirmation_message` : `str`\n\n### My Reviews Page\n- **URL Path:** `/my_reviews`\n- **Function Name:** `my_reviews_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `my_reviews.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` : `dict` (minimally `book_id`, `title`)\n  - `existing_review` : `dict` or `None` (if editing) with:\n    - `review_id` : `int`\n    - `rating` : `int`\n    - `review_text` : `str`\n\n### Submit Review Processing\n- **URL Path:** `/submit_review/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `submit_review`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Confirmation or redirect\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `confirmation_message` : `str`\n\n### User Profile Page\n- **URL Path:** `/profile`\n- **Function Name:** `profile_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET, POST\n- **Template Rendered:** `profile.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `username` : `str`\n  - `email` : `str`\n  - `borrow_history` : `list` of `dict` containing:\n    - `book_title` : `str`\n    - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `return_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD or empty)\n\n### Payment Confirmation Page\n- **URL Path:** `/payment/<int:fine_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `payment_confirmation_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET, POST\n- **Template Rendered:** `payment_confirmation.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`\n  - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`\n\n### 2. books.txt\n- **Path:** `data/books.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `title` (str)\n  3. `author` (str)\n  4. `isbn` (str)\n  5. `genre` (str)\n  6. `publisher` (str)\n  7. `year` (int)\n  8. `description` (str)\n  9. `status` (str) - Values: Available, Borrowed, Reserved\n  10. `avg_rating` (float)\n- **Description:** Stores detailed book information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`\n  - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`\n  - `3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7`\n  - `4|The Selfish Gene|Richard Dawkins|978-0-19-286092-7|Science|Oxford University Press|1976|Gene-centered view of evolution.|Reserved|4.5`\n  - `5|Steve Jobs|Walter Isaacson|978-1-4516-4853-9|Biography|Simon & Schuster|2011|Biography of Apple co-founder.|Available|4.3`\n\n### 3. borrowings.txt\n- **Path:** `data/borrowings.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `borrow_id` (int)\n  2. `username` (str)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `borrow_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n  5. `due_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n  6. `return_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD or empty)\n  7. `status` (str) - Values: Active, Returned, Overdue\n  8. `fine_amount` (float)\n- **Description:** Records book borrowing instances and statuses.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`\n  - `2|jane_doe|1|2024-10-20|2024-11-03|2024-11-02|Returned|0`\n  - `3|john_reader|3|2024-10-15|2024-10-29||Overdue|5.00`\n\n### 4. reservations.txt\n- **Path:** `data/reservations.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `reservation_id` (int)\n  2. `username` (str)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `reservation_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n  5. `status` (str) - Values: Active, Cancelled\n- **Description:** User book reservations tracking.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active`\n  - `2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled`\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- **Path:** `data/reviews.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `review_id` (int)\n  2. `username` (str)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `rating` (int 1-5)\n  5. `review_text` (str)\n  6. `review_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n- **Description:** Stores user reviews for books.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! A must-read.|2024-11-03`\n  - `2|john_reader|3|4|Thought-provoking and eerily relevant today.|2024-10-20`\n\n### 6. fines.txt\n- **Path:** `data/fines.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `fine_id` (int)\n  2. `username` (str)\n  3. `borrow_id` (int)\n  4. `amount` (float)\n  5. `status` (str) - Values: Unpaid, Paid\n  6. `date_issued` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n- **Description:** Records overdue fines issued.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|john_reader|3|5.00|Unpaid|2024-10-30`\n\n---\n\nThis document fully specifies the backend Flask routes, frontend HTML templates, and local text file data schemas needed for the OnlineLibrary application development, enabling independent parallel work by backend and frontend teams.",

        "before": "# OnlineLibrary Web Application - Design Specification\n\n---\n\n## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend Development)\n\n### Root Route\n- **URL Path:** `/`\n- **Function Name:** `root_redirect`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** None (Redirect)\n- **Description:** Redirects to the Dashboard page.\n\n### Dashboard Page\n- **URL Path:** `/dashboard`\n- **Function Name:** `dashboard_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `username` : `str` (current logged-in username)\n\n### Book Catalog Page\n- **URL Path:** `/catalog`\n- **Function Name:** `book_catalog_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` : `list` of `dict` containing:\n    - `book_id` : `int`\n    - `title` : `str`\n    - `author` : `str`\n    - `isbn` : `str`\n    - `genre` : `str`\n    - `publisher` : `str`\n    - `year` : `int`\n    - `description` : `str`\n    - `status` : `str` (\"Available\", \"Borrowed\", \"Reserved\")\n    - `avg_rating` : `float`\n\n### Book Details Page\n- **URL Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `book_details_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` : `dict` with same fields as in catalog (see above)\n  - `reviews` : `list` of `dict` containing:\n    - `review_id` : `int`\n    - `username` : `str`\n    - `rating` : `int`\n    - `review_text` : `str`\n    - `review_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)\n\n### Borrow Confirmation Page\n- **URL Path:** `/borrow/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `borrow_confirmation_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET, POST\n- **Template Rendered:** `borrow_confirmation.html`\n- **Context Variables (GET):**\n  - `book` : `dict` (minimally `book_id`, `title`, `author`)\n  - `due_date` : `str` (date 14 days from borrow date, YYYY-MM-DD)\n- **POST Processing:**\n  - Processes borrow confirmation\n  - On success, redirect or render confirmation with borrow details\n\n### My Borrowings Page\n- **URL Path:** `/my_borrows`\n- **Function Name:** `my_borrows_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `my_borrows.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `borrows` : `list` of `dict` containing:\n    - `borrow_id` : `int`\n    - `book_title` : `str`\n    - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `due_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `status` : `str` (\"Active\", \"Returned\", \"Overdue\")\n    - `fine_amount` : `float`\n\n### Return Book Route\n- **URL Path:** `/return_borrow/<int:borrow_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `return_borrow`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** `return_confirmation.html` (or redirect)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `borrow_id` : `int`\n  - `book_title` : `str`\n  - `return_date` : `str` (current date, YYYY-MM-DD)\n  - `confirmation_message` : `str`\n\n### My Reservations Page\n- **URL Path:** `/my_reservations`\n- **Function Name:** `my_reservations_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `my_reservations.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reservations` : `list` of `dict` containing:\n    - `reservation_id` : `int`\n    - `book_title` : `str`\n    - `reservation_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `status` : `str` (\"Active\", \"Cancelled\")\n\n### Cancel Reservation Route\n- **URL Path:** `/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `cancel_reservation`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Confirmation or redirect\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reservation_id` : `int`\n  - `confirmation_message` : `str`\n\n### My Reviews Page\n- **URL Path:** `/my_reviews`\n- **Function Name:** `my_reviews_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET\n- **Template Rendered:** `my_reviews.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` : `list` of `dict` containing:\n    - `review_id` : `int`\n    - `book_title` : `str`\n    - `rating` : `int`\n    - `review_text` : `str`\n    - `review_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)\n\n### Write Review Page\n- **URL Path:** `/write_review/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `write_review_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET, POST\n- **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`\n- **Context Variables (GET):**\n  - `book` : `dict` (minimally `book_id`, `title`)\n  - `existing_review` : `dict` or `None` (if editing) with:\n    - `review_id` : `int`\n    - `rating` : `int`\n    - `review_text` : `str`\n\n### Submit Review Processing\n- **URL Path:** `/submit_review/<int:book_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `submit_review`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Confirmation or redirect\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `confirmation_message` : `str`\n\n### User Profile Page\n- **URL Path:** `/profile`\n- **Function Name:** `profile_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET, POST\n- **Template Rendered:** `profile.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `username` : `str`\n  - `email` : `str`\n  - `borrow_history` : `list` of `dict` containing:\n    - `book_title` : `str`\n    - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)\n    - `return_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD or empty)\n\n### Payment Confirmation Page\n- **URL Path:** `/payment/<int:fine_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `payment_confirmation_page`\n- **HTTP Method:** GET, POST\n- **Template Rendered:** `payment_confirmation.html`\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `fine` : `dict` containing:\n    - `fine_id` : `int`\n    - `amount` : `float`\n  - Optional: `confirmation_message` : `str` on POST\n\n### Confirm Payment Processing\n- **URL Path:** `/confirm_payment/<int:fine_id>`\n- **Function Name:** `confirm_payment`\n- **HTTP Method:** POST\n- **Template Rendered:** Confirmation or redirect\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `confirmation_message` : `str`\n\n---\n\n## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications (Frontend Development)\n\n### 1. dashboard.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/dashboard.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"Library Dashboard\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `dashboard-page` (div)\n  - `welcome-message` (h1)\n  - `browse-books-button` (button)\n  - `my-borrows-button` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `username` : `str`\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `browse-books-button` → `url_for('book_catalog_page')`\n  - `my-borrows-button` → `url_for('my_borrows_page')`\n\n### 2. catalog.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/catalog.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"Book Catalog\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `catalog-page` (div)\n  - `search-input` (input)\n  - `book-grid` (div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n  - Per book:\n    - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `books` : list of dict (as described in Section 1)\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`\n  - `view-book-button-{book_id}` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`\n\n### 3. book_details.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/book_details.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"Book Details\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `book-details-page` (div)\n  - `book-title` (h1)\n  - `book-author` (div)\n  - `book-status` (div)\n  - `borrow-button` (button)\n  - `reviews-section` (div)\n  - `write-review-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-catalog` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` : dict\n  - `reviews` : list of dict\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `borrow-button` → `url_for('borrow_confirmation_page', book_id=book.book_id)`\n  - `write-review-button` → `url_for('write_review_page', book_id=book.book_id)`\n  - `back-to-catalog` → `url_for('book_catalog_page')`\n\n### 4. borrow_confirmation.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/borrow_confirmation.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"Borrow Confirmation\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `borrow-page` (div)\n  - `borrow-book-info` (div)\n  - `due-date-display` (div)\n  - `confirm-borrow-button` (button)\n  - `cancel-borrow-button` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` : dict\n  - `due_date` : str\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `cancel-borrow-button` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`\n\n### 5. my_borrows.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/my_borrows.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"My Borrowings\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `my-borrows-page` (div)\n  - `filter-status` (dropdown)\n  - `borrows-table` (table)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n  - Per borrow in `borrows`:\n    - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `borrows` : list of dict\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`\n  - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` submits POST to `url_for('return_borrow', borrow_id=borrow.borrow_id)`\n\n### 6. my_reservations.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/my_reservations.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"My Reservations\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reservations-page` (div)\n  - `reservations-table` (table)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n  - Per reservation:\n    - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reservations` : list of dict\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`\n  - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` submits POST to `url_for('cancel_reservation', reservation_id=reservation.reservation_id)`\n\n### 7. my_reviews.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/my_reviews.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"My Reviews\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `reviews-page` (div)\n  - `reviews-list` (div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n  - Per review:\n    - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` (button)\n    - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `reviews` : list of dict\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`\n  - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` → `url_for('write_review_page', book_id=review.book_id)` (the associated book)\n  - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` submits POST to a delete route with `review_id`\n\n### 8. write_review.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/write_review.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"Write Review\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `write-review-page` (div)\n  - `book-info-display` (div)\n  - `rating-input` (dropdown)\n  - `review-text` (textarea)\n  - `submit-review-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-book` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `book` : dict\n  - `existing_review` : dict or None\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-book` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`\n\n### 9. profile.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/profile.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"My Profile\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `profile-page` (div)\n  - `profile-username` (div)\n  - `profile-email` (input)\n  - `update-profile-button` (button)\n  - `borrow-history` (div)\n  - `back-to-dashboard` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `username` : `str`\n  - `email` : `str`\n  - `borrow_history` : list of dict {book_title: str, borrow_date: str, return_date: str}\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`\n\n### 10. payment_confirmation.html\n- **Filename/Path:** `templates/payment_confirmation.html`\n- **Page Title:** \"Payment Confirmation\"\n- **Element IDs:**\n  - `payment-page` (div)\n  - `fine-amount-display` (div)\n  - `confirm-payment-button` (button)\n  - `back-to-profile` (button)\n- **Context Variables:**\n  - `fine` : dict\n  - Optional: `confirmation_message` : str\n- **Navigation Mappings:**\n  - `back-to-profile` → `url_for('profile_page')`\n\n---\n\n## Section 3: Data File Schemas (Backend Development)\n\n### 1. users.txt\n- **Path:** `data/users.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `username` (str)\n  2. `email` (str)\n  3. `phone` (str)\n  4. `address` (str)\n- **Description:** Stores user profile information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`\n  - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`\n\n### 2. books.txt\n- **Path:** `data/books.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `book_id` (int)\n  2. `title` (str)\n  3. `author` (str)\n  4. `isbn` (str)\n  5. `genre` (str)\n  6. `publisher` (str)\n  7. `year` (int)\n  8. `description` (str)\n  9. `status` (str) - Values: Available, Borrowed, Reserved\n  10. `avg_rating` (float)\n- **Description:** Stores detailed book information.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`\n  - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`\n  - `3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7`\n  - `4|The Selfish Gene|Richard Dawkins|978-0-19-286092-7|Science|Oxford University Press|1976|Gene-centered view of evolution.|Reserved|4.5`\n  - `5|Steve Jobs|Walter Isaacson|978-1-4516-4853-9|Biography|Simon & Schuster|2011|Biography of Apple co-founder.|Available|4.3`\n\n### 3. borrowings.txt\n- **Path:** `data/borrowings.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `borrow_id` (int)\n  2. `username` (str)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `borrow_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n  5. `due_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n  6. `return_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD or empty)\n  7. `status` (str) - Values: Active, Returned, Overdue\n  8. `fine_amount` (float)\n- **Description:** Records book borrowing instances and statuses.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`\n  - `2|jane_doe|1|2024-10-20|2024-11-03|2024-11-02|Returned|0`\n  - `3|john_reader|3|2024-10-15|2024-10-29||Overdue|5.00`\n\n### 4. reservations.txt\n- **Path:** `data/reservations.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `reservation_id` (int)\n  2. `username` (str)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `reservation_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n  5. `status` (str) - Values: Active, Cancelled\n- **Description:** User book reservations tracking.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active`\n  - `2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled`\n\n### 5. reviews.txt\n- **Path:** `data/reviews.txt`\n- **Fields (pipe `|` delimited):**\n  1. `review_id` (int)\n  2. `username` (str)\n  3. `book_id` (int)\n  4. `rating` (int 1-5)\n  5. `review_text` (str)\n  6. `review_date` (str, YYYY-MM-DD)\n- **Description:** Stores user reviews for books.\n- **Example Rows:**\n  - `1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece!       📄 Before (full content):
         Implement app.py using design_spec.md Sections 1 and 3 for backend
         === design_spec.md ===
         # OnlineLibrary Web Application - Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend Development)
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - **URL Path:** `/`
         - **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to `/dashboard`)
         - **Context Variables:** None
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - **URL Path:** `/dashboard`
         - **Function Name:** `dashboard_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `username` : `str` (current user's username)
         
         ### 3. Book Catalog Page
         - **URL Path:** `/catalog`
         - **Function Name:** `book_catalog_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `books` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `book_id` : `int`
             - `title` : `str`
             - `author` : `str`
             - `isbn` : `str`
             - `genre` : `str`
             - `publisher` : `str`
             - `year` : `int`
             - `description` : `str`
             - `status` : `str` (Values: Available, Borrowed, Reserved)
             - `avg_rating` : `float`
         
         ### 4. Book Details Page
         - **URL Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `book_details_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `book` : `dict` (same keys as catalog books)
           - `reviews` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
              - `review_id` : `int`
              - `username` : `str`
              - `rating` : `int`
              - `review_text` : `str`
              - `review_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
         
         ### 5. Borrow Confirmation Page
         - **URL Path:** `/borrow/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `borrow_confirmation_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `borrow_confirmation.html`
         - **Context Variables (GET):**
           - `book` : `dict` (keys: `book_id`, `title`, `author`)
           - `due_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD, 14 days from borrow)
         - **POST Handling:**
           - Confirm borrowing, process logic
         
         ### 6. Borrow Confirmation Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/confirm_borrow/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `confirm_borrow`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:** Confirmation details
         
         ### 7. My Borrowings Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_borrows`
         - **Function Name:** `my_borrows_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_borrows.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `borrows` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `borrow_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `due_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `status` : `str` (All, Active, Returned, Overdue)
             - `fine_amount` : `float`
         
         ### 8. Return Book Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/return_borrow/<int:borrow_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `return_borrow`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Return confirmation or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `borrow_id` : `int`
           - `book_title` : `str`
           - `return_date` : `str` (current date)
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 9. My Reservations Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_reservations`
         - **Function Name:** `my_reservations_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_reservations.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reservations` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `reservation_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `reservation_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `status` : `str` (Active, Cancelled)
         
         ### 10. Cancel Reservation Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `cancel_reservation`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reservation_id` : `int`
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 11. My Reviews Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_reviews`
         - **Function Name:** `my_reviews_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_reviews.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reviews` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `review_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `rating` : `int`
             - `review_text` : `str`
             - `review_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
         
         ### 12. Write Review Page
         - **URL Path:** `/write_review/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `write_review_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`
         - **Context Variables (GET):**
           - `book` : `dict` (keys: `book_id`, `title`)
           - `existing_review` : `dict` or `None` (keys: `review_id`, `rating`, `review_text`)
         
         ### 13. Submit Review Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/submit_review/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `submit_review`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 14. User Profile Page
         - **URL Path:** `/profile`
         - **Function Name:** `profile_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `profile.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `username` : `str`
           - `email` : `str`
           - `borrow_history` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `return_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD or empty)
         
         ### 15. Payment Confirmation Page
         - **URL Path:** `/payment/<int:fine_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `payment_confirmation_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `payment_confirmation.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `fine` : `dict` (keys: `fine_id`, `amount`)
           - Optional `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 16. Confirm Payment Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/confirm_payment/<int:fine_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `confirm_payment`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications
         
         ### Template: `dashboard.html`
         - Path: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: "Library Dashboard"
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (div)
           - `welcome-message` (h1)
           - `browse-books-button` (button)
           - `my-borrows-button` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` : `str`
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `browse-books-button` → `url_for('book_catalog_page')`
           - `my-borrows-button` → `url_for('my_borrows_page')`
         
         ### Template: `catalog.html`
         - Path: `templates/catalog.html`
         - Page Title: "Book Catalog"
         - Element IDs:
           - `catalog-page` (div)
           - `search-input` (input)
           - `book-grid` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per book:
             - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `books` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
         
         ### Template: `book_details.html`
         - Path: `templates/book_details.html`
         - Page Title: "Book Details"
         - Element IDs:
           - `book-details-page` (div)
           - `book-title` (h1)
           - `book-author` (div)
           - `book-status` (div)
           - `borrow-button` (button)
           - `reviews-section` (div)
           - `write-review-button` (button)
           - `back-to-catalog` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `reviews` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `borrow-button` → `url_for('borrow_confirmation_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `write-review-button` → `url_for('write_review_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `back-to-catalog` → `url_for('book_catalog_page')`
         
         ### Template: `borrow_confirmation.html`
         - Path: `templates/borrow_confirmation.html`
         - Page Title: "Borrow Confirmation"
         - Element IDs:
           - `borrow-page` (div)
           - `borrow-book-info` (div)
           - `due-date-display` (div)
           - `confirm-borrow-button` (button)
           - `cancel-borrow-button` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `due_date` : str
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `cancel-borrow-button` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `confirm-borrow-button` is form submit button POSTing confirmation
         
         ### Template: `my_borrows.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_borrows.html`
         - Page Title: "My Borrowings"
         - Element IDs:
           - `my-borrows-page` (div)
           - `filter-status` (dropdown)
           - `borrows-table` (table)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per borrow:
             - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `borrows` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` POSTs to `url_for('return_borrow', borrow_id=borrow.borrow_id)`
         
         ### Template: `my_reservations.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_reservations.html`
         - Page Title: "My Reservations"
         - Element IDs:
           - `reservations-page` (div)
           - `reservations-table` (table)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per reservation:
             - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `reservations` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` POSTs to `url_for('cancel_reservation', reservation_id=reservation.reservation_id)`
         
         ### Template: `my_reviews.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_reviews.html`
         - Page Title: "My Reviews"
         - Element IDs:
           - `reviews-page` (div)
           - `reviews-list` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per review:
             - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` (button)
             - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `reviews` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` → `url_for('write_review_page', book_id=review.book_id)`
           - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` POSTs to delete review route with `review_id`
         
         ### Template: `write_review.html`
         - Path: `templates/write_review.html`
         - Page Title: "Write Review"
         - Element IDs:
           - `write-review-page` (div)
           - `book-info-display` (div)
           - `rating-input` (dropdown)
           - `review-text` (textarea)
           - `submit-review-button` (button)
           - `back-to-book` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `existing_review` : dict or None
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-book` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - Form POST submission for review
         
         ### Template: `profile.html`
         - Path: `templates/profile.html`
         - Page Title: "My Profile"
         - Element IDs:
           - `profile-page` (div)
           - `profile-username` (div)
           - `profile-email` (input)
           - `update-profile-button` (button)
           - `borrow-history` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` : str
           - `email` : str
           - `borrow_history` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
         
         ### Template: `payment_confirmation.html`
         - Path: `templates/payment_confirmation.html`
         - Page Title: "Payment Confirmation"
         - Element IDs:
           - `payment-page` (div)
           - `fine-amount-display` (div)
           - `confirm-payment-button` (button)
           - `back-to-profile` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `fine` : dict
           - Optional `confirmation_message` : str
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-profile` → `url_for('profile_page')`
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. `data/users.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `username` (str)
           2. `email` (str)
           3. `phone` (str)
           4. `address` (str)
         - Description: User profile information.
         - Examples:
           - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`
           - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`
         
         ### 2. `data/books.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `title` (str)
           3. `author` (str)
           4. `isbn` (str)
           5. `genre` (str)
           6. `publisher` (str)
           7. `year` (int)
           8. `description` (str)
           9. `status` (str: Available, Borrowed, Reserved)
           10. `avg_rating` (float)
         - Description: Book details.
         - Examples:
           - `1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`
           - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`
           - `3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7`
           - `4|The Selfish Gene|Richard Dawkins|978-0-19-286092-7|Science|Oxford University Press|1976|Gene-centered view of evolution.|Reserved|4.5`
           - `5|Steve Jobs|Walter Isaacson|978-1-4516-4853-9|Biography|Simon & Schuster|2011|Biography of Apple co-founder.|Available|4.3`
         
         ### 3. `data/borrowings.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `borrow_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `borrow_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           5. `due_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           6. `return_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD or empty)
           7. `status` (str: Active, Returned, Overdue)
           8. `fine_amount` (float)
         - Description: Records of user book borrowings.
         - Examples:
           - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`
           - `2|jane_doe|1|2024-10-20|2024-11-03|2024-11-02|Returned|0`
           - `3|john_reader|3|2024-10-15|2024-10-29||Overdue|5.00`
         
         ### 4. `data/reservations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `reservation_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `reservation_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           5. `status` (str: Active, Cancelled)
         - Description: Tracks reservations of books by users.
         - Examples:
           - `1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active`
           - `2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled`
         
         ### 5. `data/reviews.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `rating` (int from 1 to 5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: User-written book reviews.
         - Examples:
           - `1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! A must-read.|2024-11-03`
           - `2|john_reader|3|4|Thought-provoking and eerily relevant today.|2024-10-20`
         
         ### 6. `data/fines.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `fine_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `borrow_id` (int)
           4. `amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str: Unpaid, Paid)
           6. `date_issued` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Records of fines for overdue borrowings.
         - Examples:
           - `1|john_reader|3|5.00|Unpaid|2024-10-30`
         
         ---
         
         This detailed design specification document establishes the complete blueprint for the 'OnlineLibrary' application backend routes, frontend templates, and local file data structures. This enables efficient, unambiguous development by separate teams.

         using 3 backend

         === design_spec.md ===
         # OnlineLibrary Web Application - Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend Development)
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - **URL Path:** `/`
         - **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to `/dashboard`)
         - **Context Variables:** None
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - **URL Path:** `/dashboard`
         - **Function Name:** `dashboard_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `username` : `str` (current user's username)
         
         ### 3. Book Catalog Page
         - **URL Path:** `/catalog`
         - **Function Name:** `book_catalog_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `books` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `book_id` : `int`
             - `title` : `str`
             - `author` : `str`
             - `isbn` : `str`
             - `genre` : `str`
             - `publisher` : `str`
             - `year` : `int`
             - `description` : `str`
             - `status` : `str` (Values: Available, Borrowed, Reserved)
             - `avg_rating` : `float`
         
         ### 4. Book Details Page
         - **URL Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `book_details_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `book` : `dict` (same keys as catalog books)
           - `reviews` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
              - `review_id` : `int`
              - `username` : `str`
              - `rating` : `int`
              - `review_text` : `str`
              - `review_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
         
         ### 5. Borrow Confirmation Page
         - **URL Path:** `/borrow/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `borrow_confirmation_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `borrow_confirmation.html`
         - **Context Variables (GET):**
           - `book` : `dict` (keys: `book_id`, `title`, `author`)
           - `due_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD, 14 days from borrow)
         - **POST Handling:**
           - Confirm borrowing, process logic
         
         ### 6. Borrow Confirmation Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/confirm_borrow/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `confirm_borrow`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:** Confirmation details
         
         ### 7. My Borrowings Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_borrows`
         - **Function Name:** `my_borrows_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_borrows.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `borrows` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `borrow_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `due_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `status` : `str` (All, Active, Returned, Overdue)
             - `fine_amount` : `float`
         
         ### 8. Return Book Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/return_borrow/<int:borrow_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `return_borrow`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Return confirmation or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `borrow_id` : `int`
           - `book_title` : `str`
           - `return_date` : `str` (current date)
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 9. My Reservations Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_reservations`
         - **Function Name:** `my_reservations_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_reservations.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reservations` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `reservation_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `reservation_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `status` : `str` (Active, Cancelled)
         
         ### 10. Cancel Reservation Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `cancel_reservation`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reservation_id` : `int`
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 11. My Reviews Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_reviews`
         - **Function Name:** `my_reviews_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_reviews.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reviews` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `review_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `rating` : `int`
             - `review_text` : `str`
             - `review_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
         
         ### 12. Write Review Page
         - **URL Path:** `/write_review/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `write_review_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`
         - **Context Variables (GET):**
           - `book` : `dict` (keys: `book_id`, `title`)
           - `existing_review` : `dict` or `None` (keys: `review_id`, `rating`, `review_text`)
         
         ### 13. Submit Review Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/submit_review/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `submit_review`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 14. User Profile Page
         - **URL Path:** `/profile`
         - **Function Name:** `profile_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `profile.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `username` : `str`
           - `email` : `str`
           - `borrow_history` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `return_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD or empty)
         
         ### 15. Payment Confirmation Page
         - **URL Path:** `/payment/<int:fine_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `payment_confirmation_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `payment_confirmation.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `fine` : `dict` (keys: `fine_id`, `amount`)
           - Optional `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 16. Confirm Payment Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/confirm_payment/<int:fine_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `confirm_payment`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications
         
         ### Template: `dashboard.html`
         - Path: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: "Library Dashboard"
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (div)
           - `welcome-message` (h1)
           - `browse-books-button` (button)
           - `my-borrows-button` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` : `str`
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `browse-books-button` → `url_for('book_catalog_page')`
           - `my-borrows-button` → `url_for('my_borrows_page')`
         
         ### Template: `catalog.html`
         - Path: `templates/catalog.html`
         - Page Title: "Book Catalog"
         - Element IDs:
           - `catalog-page` (div)
           - `search-input` (input)
           - `book-grid` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per book:
             - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `books` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
         
         ### Template: `book_details.html`
         - Path: `templates/book_details.html`
         - Page Title: "Book Details"
         - Element IDs:
           - `book-details-page` (div)
           - `book-title` (h1)
           - `book-author` (div)
           - `book-status` (div)
           - `borrow-button` (button)
           - `reviews-section` (div)
           - `write-review-button` (button)
           - `back-to-catalog` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `reviews` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `borrow-button` → `url_for('borrow_confirmation_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `write-review-button` → `url_for('write_review_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `back-to-catalog` → `url_for('book_catalog_page')`
         
         ### Template: `borrow_confirmation.html`
         - Path: `templates/borrow_confirmation.html`
         - Page Title: "Borrow Confirmation"
         - Element IDs:
           - `borrow-page` (div)
           - `borrow-book-info` (div)
           - `due-date-display` (div)
           - `confirm-borrow-button` (button)
           - `cancel-borrow-button` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `due_date` : str
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `cancel-borrow-button` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `confirm-borrow-button` is form submit button POSTing confirmation
         
         ### Template: `my_borrows.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_borrows.html`
         - Page Title: "My Borrowings"
         - Element IDs:
           - `my-borrows-page` (div)
           - `filter-status` (dropdown)
           - `borrows-table` (table)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per borrow:
             - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `borrows` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` POSTs to `url_for('return_borrow', borrow_id=borrow.borrow_id)`
         
         ### Template: `my_reservations.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_reservations.html`
         - Page Title: "My Reservations"
         - Element IDs:
           - `reservations-page` (div)
           - `reservations-table` (table)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per reservation:
             - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `reservations` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` POSTs to `url_for('cancel_reservation', reservation_id=reservation.reservation_id)`
         
         ### Template: `my_reviews.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_reviews.html`
         - Page Title: "My Reviews"
         - Element IDs:
           - `reviews-page` (div)
           - `reviews-list` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per review:
             - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` (button)
             - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `reviews` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` → `url_for('write_review_page', book_id=review.book_id)`
           - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` POSTs to delete review route with `review_id`
         
         ### Template: `write_review.html`
         - Path: `templates/write_review.html`
         - Page Title: "Write Review"
         - Element IDs:
           - `write-review-page` (div)
           - `book-info-display` (div)
           - `rating-input` (dropdown)
           - `review-text` (textarea)
           - `submit-review-button` (button)
           - `back-to-book` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `existing_review` : dict or None
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-book` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - Form POST submission for review
         
         ### Template: `profile.html`
         - Path: `templates/profile.html`
         - Page Title: "My Profile"
         - Element IDs:
           - `profile-page` (div)
           - `profile-username` (div)
           - `profile-email` (input)
           - `update-profile-button` (button)
           - `borrow-history` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` : str
           - `email` : str
           - `borrow_history` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
         
         ### Template: `payment_confirmation.html`
         - Path: `templates/payment_confirmation.html`
         - Page Title: "Payment Confirmation"
         - Element IDs:
           - `payment-page` (div)
           - `fine-amount-display` (div)
           - `confirm-payment-button` (button)
           - `back-to-profile` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `fine` : dict
           - Optional `confirmation_message` : str
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-profile` → `url_for('profile_page')`
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. `data/users.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `username` (str)
           2. `email` (str)
           3. `phone` (str)
           4. `address` (str)
         - Description: User profile information.
         - Examples:
           - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`
           - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`
         
         ### 2. `data/books.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `title` (str)
           3. `author` (str)
           4. `isbn` (str)
           5. `genre` (str)
           6. `publisher` (str)
           7. `year` (int)
           8. `description` (str)
           9. `status` (str: Available, Borrowed, Reserved)
           10. `avg_rating` (float)
         - Description: Book details.
         - Examples:
           - `1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`
           - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`
           - `3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7`
           - `4|The Selfish Gene|Richard Dawkins|978-0-19-286092-7|Science|Oxford University Press|1976|Gene-centered view of evolution.|Reserved|4.5`
           - `5|Steve Jobs|Walter Isaacson|978-1-4516-4853-9|Biography|Simon & Schuster|2011|Biography of Apple co-founder.|Available|4.3`
         
         ### 3. `data/borrowings.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `borrow_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `borrow_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           5. `due_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           6. `return_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD or empty)
           7. `status` (str: Active, Returned, Overdue)
           8. `fine_amount` (float)
         - Description: Records of user book borrowings.
         - Examples:
           - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`
           - `2|jane_doe|1|2024-10-20|2024-11-03|2024-11-02|Returned|0`
           - `3|john_reader|3|2024-10-15|2024-10-29||Overdue|5.00`
         
         ### 4. `data/reservations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `reservation_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `reservation_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           5. `status` (str: Active, Cancelled)
         - Description: Tracks reservations of books by users.
         - Examples:
           - `1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active`
           - `2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled`
         
         ### 5. `data/reviews.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `rating` (int from 1 to 5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: User-written book reviews.
         - Examples:
           - `1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! A must-read.|2024-11-03`
           - `2|john_reader|3|4|Thought-provoking and eerily relevant today.|2024-10-20`
         
         ### 6. `data/fines.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `fine_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `borrow_id` (int)
           4. `amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str: Unpaid, Paid)
           6. `date_issued` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Records of fines for overdue borrowings.
         - Examples:
           - `1|john_reader|3|5.00|Unpaid|2024-10-30`
         
         ---
         
         This detailed design specification document establishes the complete blueprint for the 'OnlineLibrary' application backend routes, frontend templates, and local file data structures. This enables efficient, unambiguous development by separate teams.

         === design_spec.md ===
         # OnlineLibrary Web Application - Design Specification
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 1: Flask Routes Specification (Backend Development)
         
         ### 1. Root Route
         - **URL Path:** `/`
         - **Function Name:** `root_redirect`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** None (redirect to `/dashboard`)
         - **Context Variables:** None
         
         ### 2. Dashboard Page
         - **URL Path:** `/dashboard`
         - **Function Name:** `dashboard_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `dashboard.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `username` : `str` (current user's username)
         
         ### 3. Book Catalog Page
         - **URL Path:** `/catalog`
         - **Function Name:** `book_catalog_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `catalog.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `books` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `book_id` : `int`
             - `title` : `str`
             - `author` : `str`
             - `isbn` : `str`
             - `genre` : `str`
             - `publisher` : `str`
             - `year` : `int`
             - `description` : `str`
             - `status` : `str` (Values: Available, Borrowed, Reserved)
             - `avg_rating` : `float`
         
         ### 4. Book Details Page
         - **URL Path:** `/book/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `book_details_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `book_details.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `book` : `dict` (same keys as catalog books)
           - `reviews` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
              - `review_id` : `int`
              - `username` : `str`
              - `rating` : `int`
              - `review_text` : `str`
              - `review_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
         
         ### 5. Borrow Confirmation Page
         - **URL Path:** `/borrow/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `borrow_confirmation_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `borrow_confirmation.html`
         - **Context Variables (GET):**
           - `book` : `dict` (keys: `book_id`, `title`, `author`)
           - `due_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD, 14 days from borrow)
         - **POST Handling:**
           - Confirm borrowing, process logic
         
         ### 6. Borrow Confirmation Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/confirm_borrow/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `confirm_borrow`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:** Confirmation details
         
         ### 7. My Borrowings Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_borrows`
         - **Function Name:** `my_borrows_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_borrows.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `borrows` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `borrow_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `due_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `status` : `str` (All, Active, Returned, Overdue)
             - `fine_amount` : `float`
         
         ### 8. Return Book Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/return_borrow/<int:borrow_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `return_borrow`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Return confirmation or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `borrow_id` : `int`
           - `book_title` : `str`
           - `return_date` : `str` (current date)
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 9. My Reservations Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_reservations`
         - **Function Name:** `my_reservations_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_reservations.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reservations` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `reservation_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `reservation_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `status` : `str` (Active, Cancelled)
         
         ### 10. Cancel Reservation Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `cancel_reservation`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reservation_id` : `int`
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 11. My Reviews Page
         - **URL Path:** `/my_reviews`
         - **Function Name:** `my_reviews_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET
         - **Template Rendered:** `my_reviews.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `reviews` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `review_id` : `int`
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `rating` : `int`
             - `review_text` : `str`
             - `review_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
         
         ### 12. Write Review Page
         - **URL Path:** `/write_review/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `write_review_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `write_review.html`
         - **Context Variables (GET):**
           - `book` : `dict` (keys: `book_id`, `title`)
           - `existing_review` : `dict` or `None` (keys: `review_id`, `rating`, `review_text`)
         
         ### 13. Submit Review Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/submit_review/<int:book_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `submit_review`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 14. User Profile Page
         - **URL Path:** `/profile`
         - **Function Name:** `profile_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `profile.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `username` : `str`
           - `email` : `str`
           - `borrow_history` : `list` of `dict` with keys:
             - `book_title` : `str`
             - `borrow_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD)
             - `return_date` : `str` (YYYY-MM-DD or empty)
         
         ### 15. Payment Confirmation Page
         - **URL Path:** `/payment/<int:fine_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `payment_confirmation_page`
         - **HTTP Method:** GET, POST
         - **Template Rendered:** `payment_confirmation.html`
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `fine` : `dict` (keys: `fine_id`, `amount`)
           - Optional `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ### 16. Confirm Payment Processing
         - **URL Path:** `/confirm_payment/<int:fine_id>`
         - **Function Name:** `confirm_payment`
         - **HTTP Method:** POST
         - **Template Rendered:** Confirmation page or redirect
         - **Context Variables:**
           - `confirmation_message` : `str`
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 2: HTML Template Specifications
         
         ### Template: `dashboard.html`
         - Path: `templates/dashboard.html`
         - Page Title: "Library Dashboard"
         - Element IDs:
           - `dashboard-page` (div)
           - `welcome-message` (h1)
           - `browse-books-button` (button)
           - `my-borrows-button` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` : `str`
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `browse-books-button` → `url_for('book_catalog_page')`
           - `my-borrows-button` → `url_for('my_borrows_page')`
         
         ### Template: `catalog.html`
         - Path: `templates/catalog.html`
         - Page Title: "Book Catalog"
         - Element IDs:
           - `catalog-page` (div)
           - `search-input` (input)
           - `book-grid` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per book:
             - `view-book-button-{book_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `books` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `view-book-button-{book_id}` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
         
         ### Template: `book_details.html`
         - Path: `templates/book_details.html`
         - Page Title: "Book Details"
         - Element IDs:
           - `book-details-page` (div)
           - `book-title` (h1)
           - `book-author` (div)
           - `book-status` (div)
           - `borrow-button` (button)
           - `reviews-section` (div)
           - `write-review-button` (button)
           - `back-to-catalog` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `reviews` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `borrow-button` → `url_for('borrow_confirmation_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `write-review-button` → `url_for('write_review_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `back-to-catalog` → `url_for('book_catalog_page')`
         
         ### Template: `borrow_confirmation.html`
         - Path: `templates/borrow_confirmation.html`
         - Page Title: "Borrow Confirmation"
         - Element IDs:
           - `borrow-page` (div)
           - `borrow-book-info` (div)
           - `due-date-display` (div)
           - `confirm-borrow-button` (button)
           - `cancel-borrow-button` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `due_date` : str
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `cancel-borrow-button` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - `confirm-borrow-button` is form submit button POSTing confirmation
         
         ### Template: `my_borrows.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_borrows.html`
         - Page Title: "My Borrowings"
         - Element IDs:
           - `my-borrows-page` (div)
           - `filter-status` (dropdown)
           - `borrows-table` (table)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per borrow:
             - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `borrows` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `return-book-button-{borrow_id}` POSTs to `url_for('return_borrow', borrow_id=borrow.borrow_id)`
         
         ### Template: `my_reservations.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_reservations.html`
         - Page Title: "My Reservations"
         - Element IDs:
           - `reservations-page` (div)
           - `reservations-table` (table)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per reservation:
             - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `reservations` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `cancel-reservation-button-{reservation_id}` POSTs to `url_for('cancel_reservation', reservation_id=reservation.reservation_id)`
         
         ### Template: `my_reviews.html`
         - Path: `templates/my_reviews.html`
         - Page Title: "My Reviews"
         - Element IDs:
           - `reviews-page` (div)
           - `reviews-list` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
           - Per review:
             - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` (button)
             - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `reviews` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
           - `edit-review-button-{review_id}` → `url_for('write_review_page', book_id=review.book_id)`
           - `delete-review-button-{review_id}` POSTs to delete review route with `review_id`
         
         ### Template: `write_review.html`
         - Path: `templates/write_review.html`
         - Page Title: "Write Review"
         - Element IDs:
           - `write-review-page` (div)
           - `book-info-display` (div)
           - `rating-input` (dropdown)
           - `review-text` (textarea)
           - `submit-review-button` (button)
           - `back-to-book` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `book` : dict
           - `existing_review` : dict or None
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-book` → `url_for('book_details_page', book_id=book.book_id)`
           - Form POST submission for review
         
         ### Template: `profile.html`
         - Path: `templates/profile.html`
         - Page Title: "My Profile"
         - Element IDs:
           - `profile-page` (div)
           - `profile-username` (div)
           - `profile-email` (input)
           - `update-profile-button` (button)
           - `borrow-history` (div)
           - `back-to-dashboard` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `username` : str
           - `email` : str
           - `borrow_history` : list of dict
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-dashboard` → `url_for('dashboard_page')`
         
         ### Template: `payment_confirmation.html`
         - Path: `templates/payment_confirmation.html`
         - Page Title: "Payment Confirmation"
         - Element IDs:
           - `payment-page` (div)
           - `fine-amount-display` (div)
           - `confirm-payment-button` (button)
           - `back-to-profile` (button)
         - Context Variables:
           - `fine` : dict
           - Optional `confirmation_message` : str
         - Navigation Mappings:
           - `back-to-profile` → `url_for('profile_page')`
         
         ---
         
         ## Section 3: Data File Schemas
         
         ### 1. `data/users.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `username` (str)
           2. `email` (str)
           3. `phone` (str)
           4. `address` (str)
         - Description: User profile information.
         - Examples:
           - `john_reader|john@example.com|555-1234|123 Main St`
           - `jane_doe|jane@example.com|555-5678|789 Oak St`
         
         ### 2. `data/books.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `book_id` (int)
           2. `title` (str)
           3. `author` (str)
           4. `isbn` (str)
           5. `genre` (str)
           6. `publisher` (str)
           7. `year` (int)
           8. `description` (str)
           9. `status` (str: Available, Borrowed, Reserved)
           10. `avg_rating` (float)
         - Description: Book details.
         - Examples:
           - `1|To Kill a Mockingbird|Harper Lee|978-0-06-112008-4|Fiction|HarperCollins|1960|A gripping tale of racial injustice and childhood innocence.|Available|4.8`
           - `2|Sapiens|Yuval Noah Harari|978-0-06-231609-7|Non-Fiction|Harper|2011|A brief history of humankind.|Borrowed|4.6`
           - `3|1984|George Orwell|978-0-452-28423-4|Fiction|Signet Classic|1949|A dystopian social science fiction novel.|Available|4.7`
           - `4|The Selfish Gene|Richard Dawkins|978-0-19-286092-7|Science|Oxford University Press|1976|Gene-centered view of evolution.|Reserved|4.5`
           - `5|Steve Jobs|Walter Isaacson|978-1-4516-4853-9|Biography|Simon & Schuster|2011|Biography of Apple co-founder.|Available|4.3`
         
         ### 3. `data/borrowings.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `borrow_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `borrow_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           5. `due_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           6. `return_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD or empty)
           7. `status` (str: Active, Returned, Overdue)
           8. `fine_amount` (float)
         - Description: Records of user book borrowings.
         - Examples:
           - `1|john_reader|2|2024-11-01|2024-11-15||Active|0`
           - `2|jane_doe|1|2024-10-20|2024-11-03|2024-11-02|Returned|0`
           - `3|john_reader|3|2024-10-15|2024-10-29||Overdue|5.00`
         
         ### 4. `data/reservations.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `reservation_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `reservation_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
           5. `status` (str: Active, Cancelled)
         - Description: Tracks reservations of books by users.
         - Examples:
           - `1|jane_doe|4|2024-11-10|Active`
           - `2|john_reader|2|2024-10-25|Cancelled`
         
         ### 5. `data/reviews.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `review_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `book_id` (int)
           4. `rating` (int from 1 to 5)
           5. `review_text` (str)
           6. `review_date` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: User-written book reviews.
         - Examples:
           - `1|jane_doe|1|5|An absolute masterpiece! A must-read.|2024-11-03`
           - `2|john_reader|3|4|Thought-provoking and eerily relevant today.|2024-10-20`
         
         ### 6. `data/fines.txt`
         - Fields (pipe-separated):
           1. `fine_id` (int)
           2. `username` (str)
           3. `borrow_id` (int)
           4. `amount` (float)
           5. `status` (str: Unpaid, Paid)
           6. `date_issued` (str YYYY-MM-DD)
         - Description: Records of fines for overdue borrowings.
         - Examples:
           - `1|john_reader|3|5.00|Unpaid|2024-10-30`
         
         ---
         
         This detailed design specification document establishes the complete blueprint for the 'OnlineLibrary' application backend routes, frontend templates, and local file data structures. This enables efficient, unambiguous development by separate teams.

      Type: STRESS_CHAOS_WORD_DELETION
